          player: blankSwfConfig
        };

        window.ytcfg.set('FILLER_DATA', fillerData);
      };

        window.getPageData = function() {
          if (window.ytcsi) {window.ytcsi.tick("pr", null, '');}
          var endpoint = null;
            endpoint = {"commandMetadata":{"webCommandMetadata":{"url":"/channel/UCOmHUn--16B90oW2L6FRR3A","webPageType":"WEB_PAGE_TYPE_BROWSE"}},"urlEndpoint":{"url":"/channel/UCOmHUn--16B90oW2L6FRR3A"}};
          var data = {
              page: "browse",
              player: ytplayer.config,
              playerResponse: window.ytInitialPlayerResponse,
                url: "\/channel\/UCOmHUn--16B90oW2L6FRR3A",
                csn: "x_fwXKPuPITJkwatzaPYBA",
              response: window.ytInitialData,
              endpoint: endpoint
          };
          return {
            data: data,
            endpoint: endpoint
          };
        };

        if (window.loadDataHook) {
          var pageData = window.getPageData();
          window.loadDataHook(pageData.endpoint, pageData.data);
          window.loadDataHook = null;
        }
        setFiller();

        document.title = "BLACKPINK - 'Kill This Love' M\/V - YouTube";

    })();

      var meta = document.createElement('meta');
      meta.name = 'referrer';
      meta.content = 'origin-when-cross-origin';
      document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(meta);
      var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
      var microformatContainer = document.getElementById('microformat');
      while (microformatContainer.childNodes.length > 0) {
        head.appendChild(microformatContainer.childNodes[0]);
      }
